<i>clouds</i> of steam, <b><a href="text?doc=Perseus:abo:tlg,2003,012:341d&amp;lang=original" target="_new"><span class="en">Jul.<u>Mis.</u>341d</span></a></b>; esp. of <i>odours,</i> <b><a href="text?doc=Perseus:abo:tlg,0085,005:1311&amp;lang=original" target="_new"><span class="en">A.<u>Ag.</u>1311</span></a></b>, <i><span class="en">Arist.<u>Pr.</u>908a21</span></i>, <i><span class="en">Ph.1.96</span></i>,al., <i><span class="en">Lib.<u>Or.</u>12.79</span></i> (pl.), etc.;
